FNV PBR PPLIGHTING TEXTURE PROPERTY FIELD SOURCE AUDIT

Purpose:
1. Identify the producer-side material texture fields behind PPLighting BA9EE0 resources.
2. Audit A59D30(3) property fields +0xAC..+0xC0 and BGSTextureSet +0x30 vtable +0x8C texture slots.
3. Keep native PBR blocked unless diffuse/normal/glow/etc. resource provenance reaches final SetTexture stages.
